          <div class="t withAv">
           Some headers about the campaign:
           <br/>
           <br/>
           - We have a Monk, a Barbarian(me!), a Cleric, a Paladin, and a Rogue.
           <br/>
           - The Paladin have two pet/slave/servent goblins we adquired in the last dungeon through some very sucessful Diplomacy rolls.
           <br/>
           - The Monk NEVER punches anything, he uses a homebrew lionman race that have a Shout ability, all damage he have done so far is either with that, or by throwing things, such as body parts of our latest foes, or, primarially, our Cleric.
           <br/>
           - The Monk's primary method of "healing" people is shoving copious amounts of booze down people's throats, last we checked, our Rogue was completelly
           <a class="forUnlogged" href="#" onclick="users.showLoginForm(window.location);return false;" style="display:inline" title="Register Or Login to View Text">
            *********
           </a>
           because of this.
           <br/>
           - I've made a surprising amount of sucessful Strength checks so far(not that surprising given 18 Str, but still), and I am growing a reputation within the party.
           <br/>
           - The Cleric and, surprisingly, the Barbarian are the only remotelly sane people in the party, and that number is reduced by one mid-Rage, this may change since some people are getting attached to their characteres and might start taking things a bit more serious, but still.
          </div>
